Use your eraser button on the pen to remove both ink strokes and existing notation. You can print the entire score, as well as individual parts for each musician. StaffPad has smart collision avoidance and music layout rules which handle the reflowing of the music to a page-based layout automatically.\r\n\r\nSHARE YOUR WORK\r\nStaffPad allows you to easily share and export your work. You can export MIDI and MusicXML, should you wish to continue working on your score in other programs. StaffPad also supports import of MusicXML and MIDI files.\r\n\r\nSCORE SYNC AND AUTO-SAVE\r\nStaffPad is always saving your score, and keeping track of versions - which you can return to at anytime.
